class QRHLayer(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self, embed_dim):
        self.embed_dim = embed_dim
        self.spectral_filter = SpectralFilter(alpha=1.72)

    def forward(self, x):
        # Quaternion transformation
        q = self.to_quaternion(x)
        # Spectral filtering
        q_filtered = self.spectral_filter(q)
        # Geometric rotation

        return self.from_quaternion(q_rotated)

class QRHLayer(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self, embed_dim):
        self.embed_dim = embed_dim
        self.spectral_filter = SpectralFilter(alpha=1.74)

    def forward(self, x):

        # Spectral filtering

        # Geometric rotation

        return self.from_quaternion(q_rotated)

# Î¨QRH Layer Processing
class QRHLayer(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self, embed_dim):
        self.embed_dim = embed_dim
        self.spectral_filter = SpectralFilter(alpha=1.72)

    def forward(self, x):
        # Quaternion transformation
        q = self.to_quaternion(x)
        # Spectral filtering
        q_filtered = self.spectral_filter(q)
        # Geometric rotation
        q_rotated = self.apply_rotation(q_filtered)
        return self.from_quaternion(q_rotated)

=== Implementation Details ===
```python
# Î¨QRH Layer Processing
class QRHLayer(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self, embed_dim):
        self.embed_dim = embed_dim
        self.spectral_filter = SpectralFilter(alpha=1.71)

    def forward(self, x):
        # Quaternion transformation
        q = self.to_quaternion(x)
        # Spectral filtering
        q_filtered = self.spectral_filter(q)
        # Geometric rotation
        q_rotated = self.apply_rotation(q_filtered)
        return self.from_quaternion(q_rotated)
```
